< Review>
I come to Del Taco exclusively for their buck & under value menu.  It is very disappointing when you come to a location such as this and see the price of a bean burrito at $1.49  that's a 50% inflation over the standard chain pricing that normally makes Del Taco such an incredible value (at other locations).  In addition to this, the person at the register accidentally charged me for an extra item that I didn't ask for and had to go through the hassle of refunding and recharging a new order.

The food quality was decent, the chicken roller I got was tasty.  I also tried some of the churros and they were caked in sugar, just way overdone.  I would avoid this location and hold out for other Del Tacos, even if someone tells you it's right next to Target don't believe them.</Review>

<text>Love Love LOVE this place. I'm a born hater with a frugality trait, so saying love means a lot from me. Prices, native selection, outdoor selection, fruit tree selection, service, customer service - top notch as far as I can scrutinize. I've only been to the newest location in Eastvale. From the pictures and reviews posted up about their other locations, their indoor/tropical plant selection and prices is suppose to be above the local average, but sadly my visits keep landing on the hump days their restocking times and they seem to still be setting up the greenhouse in which the tropicals are suppese to be located in. I sell tropicals/houseplants online and it becomes pricey to drive far to only buy what is still considered less than the wholesale amount. I'm moving to the Riverside/Jurupa Valley area at this moment, so this nursery + their prices being only 5 minutes away is just a dream. I support our local(ish) companies as much as I can(I try, but not to hard haha) so this nursery selling Kellogg soils(Ontario), my favorite and go to soil ammendment, is great but seems to be priced a little bit higher than say, Home Depot. I went on September 9, 2020 to those of you who are interested in Kellogg's Shade Mix: this nursery does sell it but they(like everywhere else) are waiting 3+ months to get it in stock as it seems to be something awry on Kellogg's end.

I'm a simpleton with a 4 track mind, if you don't know what this means, here's the translation: This nursery is a new favorite of mine and I'll be dragging the hubby and the baby(both of which hate dirt, heat, and feel nothing for plants) here more often than even I can forsee. So I will be sure to keep this review UTD. I'll aim to review + piccys each time I visit, but we'll see what goes.

Thanks for the read. Hope my rantings have helped some of you somehow. Otherwise, sorry you wasted your time reading this haha

Well, I have a good story 'bout this place: So we had been planning a night out to Mi Ranchito in Sonoma since they opened(a year ago apparently). However-you know about "plans well made"...anyway there was a fire, home purchase and 2 severe family illnesses that literally kept us from Mi Ranchito's front door though we basically went past it more than a few times a day. Go figure! Anyhow knowing we(son&daughter-we live together) would probably never make it at that rate, I decided to take a "bold step of my own" and look up their menu online to see what we had been missing and maybe that would get us down there in shorter order. Guess it worked cuz the menu looked soooooooo good I used the phone number on the web to call in for a pick up order: the gentleman on the phone seemed a bit hesitant as I was ordering‚Äîwhich I chalked off to heavy accents on both parts‚Äîme English‚Äîhe Spanish. But I said thank you after agreeing on a pick up time. Anyway-better cut this short(er)üòÅGot down there ONLY to find out the menu I used was NOT the Sonoma Restaurant's and virtually nothing was done. But we got it squared away. So I sat...and I sat.. BUT within 10 minutes I was handed a brown shopping bag and a receipt to sign and I left with goodies in hand(oh no he helped me to my car as I use a cane)and I was off to my home. Let me tell you that bag smelled soooooooo good it was difficult to drive home. Well we put it on plates and were completely blown away-AWESOME!!! After the first bite we ALL were simply BLOWN AWAY! Absolutely the very BEST Mexican-American food known to man! Cold, Hot or in-between simply the BEST! Thank you Mi Ranchito for a decision well made. Forget the plans and GO!!!< /text>

I'm only giving a one-star review because it's the lowest Google's got!

In the letter, it also stated that they were willing to take my braces off and would give me a retainer all for free, because if I kept them on, there was a high possibility that I would get cavities that would not be able to be taken care of until the braces are off.

Well, here is where my issue comes in. I'd called to schedule an appointment with them to have this taken care of. They'd informed me that I would need to pay $200 out of pocket to take them off. I'd mentioned the letter they sent me, but even with the letter, they'd refused to do the service for free as stated. I didn't end up making the appointment, because I didn't have $200 to just give away. So, by that point I was just willing to let it go.
